<p>In City's first game of the season, Agüero scored both goals in the 2–0 <a href="/wiki/2018_FA_Community_Shield" title="2018 FA Community Shield">2018 FA Community Shield</a> victory over Chelsea, the first goal being his 200th for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-2018CommunityShield_181-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2018CommunityShield-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> On 19 August 2018, Agüero scored his 9th Premier League hat-trick in a 6–1 home victory against <a href="/wiki/Huddersfield_Town_A.F.C." title="Huddersfield Town A.F.C.">Huddersfield Town</a>, putting him behind only <a href="/wiki/Alan_Shearer" title="Alan Shearer">Alan Shearer</a>'s 11.<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup> He also leapfrogged <a href="/wiki/Robin_van_Persie" title="Robin van Persie">Robin van Persie</a> to enter the league's top ten scorers of all time, and second place in foreign Premier League scorers only to <a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Thierry Henry</a>'s 175.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup> Agüero hit the post twice in a 1–1 away draw against <a href="/wiki/Wolverhampton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Wolverhampton Wanderers F.C.">Wolverhampton Wanderers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup> On 21 September, Manchester City confirmed via their official website that Agüero had signed a new contract with the club, keeping him at the Etihad Stadium until 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup> On 22 September, in his 300th appearance for Manchester City, Agüero scored the opening goal in an eventual 5–0 away win over Cardiff City.<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 4 November, Agüero scored his 150th Premier League goal in a 6–1 home win over Southampton, which was his 217th Premier League appearance; he became only the ninth player in history to achieve this landmark, and only the third player after Thierry Henry and <a href="/wiki/Wayne_Rooney" title="Wayne Rooney">Wayne Rooney</a> to manage this tally with a single side. He was also the second-fastest player to reach this milestone, after Alan Shearer, who took five fewer appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup> On 11 November, Agüero scored the second goal in a 3–1 win against Manchester United, making him the joint highest scorer in Manchester derbies in the Premier League era, level with <a href="/wiki/Wayne_Rooney" title="Wayne Rooney">Wayne Rooney</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup> On 29 January 2019, Agüero scored within 24 seconds in an eventual 2–1 defeat at Newcastle United.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> On 3 February, Agüero scored a hat-trick against rivals Arsenal, including one goal within 48 seconds, bringing his Premier League tally of hat-tricks to ten, in a 3–1 win at the Etihad Stadium.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup> On 10 February, Agüero scored his 11th hat-trick in the Premier League, as Manchester City defeated rivals Chelsea 6–0 at home;<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> with this feat, he equalled Alan Shearer's record of 11 in the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup> The hat trick also saw Agüero overtake <a href="/wiki/Tommy_Johnson_(footballer,_born_1901)" title="Tommy Johnson (footballer, born 1901)">Tommy Johnson's</a> and Eric Brook's record of 158 league goals for the club, and set a new record of 160 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup> The following month, he scored twice in a 7–0 (10–2 aggregate) Champions League win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Schalke_04" title="FC Schalke 04">Schalke</a> and in doing so helped the club equal the record for the largest winning margin in the knockout-phase of the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season"><a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="2019–20 Manchester City F.C. season">2019–20 season</a></span></h4>
<p>On 10 August 2019, Agüero came on as a substitute replacing Gabriel Jesus, in a match that was dominated by the newly introduced <a href="/wiki/Video_assistant_referee" title="Video assistant referee">VAR</a>, at the <a href="/wiki/London_Stadium" title="London Stadium">London Stadium</a> against <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a>. With City 3–0 up, they were awarded a penalty for a foul on <a href="/wiki/Riyad_Mahrez" title="Riyad Mahrez">Riyad Mahrez</a>. Agüero took the penalty and it was saved by opposing keeper <a href="/wiki/%C5%81ukasz_Fabia%C5%84ski" title="ukasz Fabiaski">ukasz Fabiaski</a>. However, VAR stepped in and re-awarded the penalty for an infringement by <a href="/wiki/Declan_Rice" title="Declan Rice">Declan Rice</a>. Agüero scored the re-awarded penalty in an eventual 5–0 away day opening win for the <i>Citizens</i> to start their Premier League title defence.
<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup> On 12 January 2020, Agüero scored 12th hattrick of his <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> career against <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a> in 6–1 away victory at <a href="/wiki/Villa_Park" title="Villa Park">Villa Park</a>, taking his individual tally past Thierry Henry's 175 goal mark.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Agüero scored the 399th and 400th goals of his professional career in a 3–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/A.F.C._Bournemouth" class="mw-redirect" title="A.F.C. Bournemouth">Bournemouth</a> on 25 August.<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season"><a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="2020–21 Manchester City F.C. season">2020–21 season</a></span></h4>
<p>After several weeks on the sidelines due to a <a href="/wiki/Tear_of_meniscus" title="Tear of meniscus">meniscus injury</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup> Agüero returned to action on 17 October 2020 in a 1–0 victory against Arsenal at the Etihad Stadium.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup> On 21 October 2020, he scored his first goal of the season in a 3–1 win over Porto in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League">2020–21 UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth_teams">Youth teams</span></h3>
<p>Agüero was selected for the <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_under-17_football_team" title="Argentina national under-17 football team">Argentina U17</a> team to participate at the <a href="https://es.wikipedia.org/wiki/Campeonato_Sudamericano_Sub-16_de_2004" class="extiw" title="es:Campeonato Sudamericano Sub-16 de 2004">2004 U-16 South American Championship</a> in Paraguay in September. He participated in all of Argentina's group stage matches, scoring in a 2–1 win against the <a href="/wiki/United_States_men%27s_national_under-17_soccer_team" title="United States men&#39;s national under-17 soccer team">United States</a> and a 3–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Ecuador_national_under-17_football_team" title="Ecuador national under-17 football team">Ecuador</a> to help Argentina finish top of their group. Agüero scored in the 47th minute of Argentina's 1–0 quarter-final victory against <a href="/wiki/Peru_national_under-17_football_team" title="Peru national under-17 football team">Peru</a>, setting up a semi-final match against <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_under-17_football_team" title="Colombia national under-17 football team">Colombia</a> which Argentina lost 2–0.
</p><p>Agüero represented Argentina at two <a href="/wiki/FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="FIFA U-20 World Cup">FIFA World Youth Championships</a>, winning back-to-back world titles. He was part of the team that won the <a href="/wiki/2005_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship" title="2005 FIFA World Youth Championship">2005 edition</a> in the Netherlands, alongside his future 2008 Olympics squad teammates <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Gago" title="Fernando Gago">Fernando Gago</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>. At the <a href="/wiki/2007_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2007 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2007 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a>, held in Canada, Agüero scored twice and helped set up three goals in a 6–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Panama_national_under-20_football_team" title="Panama national under-20 football team">Panama</a> in the second game of the group stage of the tournament. He then scored the only goal in Argentina's third match against <a href="/wiki/North_Korea_national_under-20_football_team" title="North Korea national under-20 football team">North Korea</a> from a free kick. Having qualified to the round of 16, he scored two of the three goals against <a href="/wiki/Poland_national_under-20_football_team" title="Poland national under-20 football team">Poland</a> that would eventually give them a <a href="/wiki/2007_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup#Round_of_16" title="2007 FIFA U-20 World Cup">3–1</a> win to advance to the next round. Argentina defeated <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_under-20_football_team" title="Mexico national under-20 football team">Mexico</a> in the quarter-finals and <a href="/wiki/Chile_national_under-20_football_team" title="Chile national under-20 football team">Chile</a> in the semi-finals, and faced the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic_national_under-20_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Czech Republic national under-20 football team">Czech Republic</a> in the finals, a team they drew <a href="/wiki/2007_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup#Group_E" title="2007 FIFA U-20 World Cup">0–0</a> in the group stage. Agüero captained and scored the equaliser in the 62nd minute, leading to a <a href="/wiki/2007_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup#Final" title="2007 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2–1</a> victory. In addition, Agüero won the Golden Boot of the tournament, scoring six goals in seven, and the Golden Ball as the best player of the tournament.
</p><p>As a member of the Argentine squad for the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2008_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2008 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">2008 Beijing Olympics</a>, Agüero scored two goals in the space of five minutes in the semi-final <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2008_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament#Semi-finals" title="Football at the 2008 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">3–0</a> win over <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_under-23_football_team" title="Brazil national under-23 football team">Brazil</a> on 19 August 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> Argentina went on to win its second consecutive gold medal at the Olympic tournament.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Senior_team">Senior team</span></h3>
<h4><span id="Debut.2C_2010_World_Cup_and_2011_Copa_Am.C3.A9rica"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Debut,_2010_World_Cup_and_2011_Copa_América">Debut, 2010 World Cup and 2011 Copa América</span></h4>
<p>At age 18, Agüero made his senior debut for <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> in a friendly with <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a>, played at <a href="/wiki/Emirates_Stadium" title="Emirates Stadium">Emirates Stadium</a>, England on 3 September 2006.<sup id="cite_ref-Official_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Official-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup> A year later, he scored his first international goal in a <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONMEBOL)" title="2010 FIFA World Cup qualification (CONMEBOL)">2010 FIFA World Cup qualification</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Bolivia_national_football_team" title="Bolivia national football team">Bolivia</a>, and went on to score three more times as the <i>Albiceleste</i> successfully qualified for the finals in <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_(L),_Ricardo_Rodriguez_(C),_Valentin_Stocker_(R)_-_Switzerland_vs._Argentina,_29th_February_2012.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_%28L%29%2C_Ricardo_Rodriguez_%28C%29%2C_Valentin_Stocker_%28R%29_-_Switzerland_vs._Argentina%2C_29th_February_2012.jpg/220px-Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_%28L%29%2C_Ricardo_Rodriguez_%28C%29%2C_Valentin_Stocker_%28R%29_-_Switzerland_vs._Argentina%2C_29th_February_2012.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_%28L%29%2C_Ricardo_Rodriguez_%28C%29%2C_Valentin_Stocker_%28R%29_-_Switzerland_vs._Argentina%2C_29th_February_2012.jpg/330px-Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_%28L%29%2C_Ricardo_Rodriguez_%28C%29%2C_Valentin_Stocker_%28R%29_-_Switzerland_vs._Argentina%2C_29th_February_2012.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_%28L%29%2C_Ricardo_Rodriguez_%28C%29%2C_Valentin_Stocker_%28R%29_-_Switzerland_vs._Argentina%2C_29th_February_2012.jpg/440px-Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_%28L%29%2C_Ricardo_Rodriguez_%28C%29%2C_Valentin_Stocker_%28R%29_-_Switzerland_vs._Argentina%2C_29th_February_2012.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4352" data-file-height="2902" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_(L),_Ricardo_Rodriguez_(C),_Valentin_Stocker_(R)_-_Switzerland_vs._Argentina,_29th_February_2012.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Agüero taking on two Swiss players in an international friendly in 2012</div></div></div>
<p>Agüero was chosen for the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a> squad, and made his <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> debut in Argentina's second group match against <a href="/wiki/Korea_Republic_national_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Korea Republic national football team">South Korea</a> on 12 June 2010, replacing <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Tevez" title="Carlos Tevez">Carlos Tevez</a> in the 75th minute. Agüero's impact was immediate as Argentina scored in the next minute. He assisted on <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Higua%C3%ADn" title="Gonzalo Higuaín">Gonzalo Higuaín</a>'s hat-trick goal late in the game. Argentina won the game <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_Group_B#Argentina_vs_Korea_Republic" title="2010 FIFA World Cup Group B">4–1</a>. Argentina, however, subsequently lost to <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Argentina_vs_Germany" title="2010 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">quarter-finals</a>.
</p><p>Agüero was named in the 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2011_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2011 Copa América">2011 Copa América</a> where Argentina had been drawn into Group A with <a href="/wiki/Bolivia_national_football_team" title="Bolivia national football team">Bolivia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Costa_Rica_national_football_team" title="Costa Rica national football team">Costa Rica</a>. On 1 July, in Argentina's opening <a href="/wiki/2011_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Group_A" title="2011 Copa América Group A">group stage</a> match against Bolivia, he came on for <a href="/wiki/Ezequiel_Lavezzi" title="Ezequiel Lavezzi">Ezequiel Lavezzi</a> on 71 minutes and scored an equaliser on 76 minutes to secure a 1–1 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup> On 11 July, in Argentina's third group stage match against Costa Rica, Agüero scored a goal in each half as Argentina won 3–0 and finished in second position in their group.<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2014_World_Cup.2C_and_2015_and_2016_Copas_Am.C3.A9rica"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2014_World_Cup,_and_2015_and_2016_Copas_América">2014 World Cup, and 2015 and 2016 Copas América</span></h4>
<p>Agüero was named in Argentina's 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup> On 15 June, he started alongside Lionel Messi as a forward in Argentina's 2–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina_national_football_team" title="Bosnia and Herzegovina national football team">Bosnia and Herzegovina</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Est%C3%A1dio_do_Maracan%C3%A3" class="mw-redirect" title="Estádio do Maracanã">Estádio do Maracanã</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Agüero was named in the Argentine squad for the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2015 Copa América">2015 Copa América</a>, and in a warm-up game on 7 June against Bolivia in <a href="/wiki/San_Juan,_Argentina" title="San Juan, Argentina">San Juan</a>, he scored his first international hat-trick in a 5–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup> On 13 June, he scored Argentina's opening goal of the tournament in a 2–2 <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Group_B" title="2015 Copa América Group B">group stage</a> draw with <a href="/wiki/Paraguay_national_football_team" title="Paraguay national football team">Paraguay</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup> Three days later at the same ground, he headed a cross from Manchester City teammate <a href="/wiki/Pablo_Zabaleta" title="Pablo Zabaleta">Pablo Zabaleta</a> for a 1–0 win against holders <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup> At the semi-final stage, Agüero headed in <a href="/wiki/%C3%81ngel_Di_Mar%C3%ADa" title="Ángel Di María">Ángel Di María</a>'s cross as Argentina defeated Paraguay 6–1 to reach the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Final" title="2015 Copa América Final">2015 Copa América Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup> Agüero started the final against <a href="/wiki/Chile_national_football_team" title="Chile national football team">Chile</a>, but was replaced in the 74th minute for Gonzalo Higuaín in an eventual penalty shootout loss.<sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Agüero was included in <a href="/wiki/Gerardo_Martino" title="Gerardo Martino">Gerardo Martino</a>'s 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Centenario" title="Copa América Centenario">Copa América Centenario</a> and scored his first goal of the tournament in Argentina's second group match, a 5–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Panama_national_football_team" title="Panama national football team">Panama</a> on 10 June 2016, which allowed them to advance to the quarter-finals of the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">&#91;216&#93;</a></sup> Agüero considered retiring from international football shortly after losing against <a href="/wiki/Chile_national_football_team" title="Chile national football team">Chile</a> in a penalty shootout in the <a href="/wiki/Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Centenario_Final" title="Copa América Centenario Final">final</a> of the tournament for a second consecutive time.<sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">&#91;217&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018_World_Cup_and_2019_Copa_Am.C3.A9rica"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_World_Cup_and_2019_Copa_América">2018 World Cup and 2019 Copa América</span></h4>
<p>On 14 November 2017, Agüero was taken to hospital after fainting in the dressing room at half-time in a 4–2 loss to <a href="/wiki/Nigeria_national_football_team" title="Nigeria national football team">Nigeria</a> in a friendly match in <a href="/wiki/Krasnodar" title="Krasnodar">Krasnodar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">&#91;218&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2018, Agüero was named in Argentina's preliminary 35-man <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">&#91;219&#93;</a></sup> later that month, he was included in <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Sampaoli" title="Jorge Sampaoli">Jorge Sampaoli</a>'s final 23-man squad for the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">&#91;220&#93;</a></sup> In his team's first group match of the tournament against <a href="/wiki/Iceland_national_football_team" title="Iceland national football team">Iceland</a> on 16 June, he scored the opening goal of an eventual 1–1 draw; this was his first ever World Cup goal.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup> In the round of 16 match against <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> on 30 June, Agüero scored Argentina's final goal in a 4–3 defeat, which saw his side eliminated from the World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 21 May 2019, he was included in <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Scaloni" title="Lionel Scaloni">Lionel Scaloni</a>'s final 23-man Argentina squad for the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-223" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-223">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup> In Argentina's final group match against <a href="/wiki/Qatar_national_football_team" title="Qatar national football team">Qatar</a> on 23 June, Agüero scored the second goal in a 2–0 win, which enabled his team to advance to the knock-out stages.<sup id="cite_ref-224" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-224">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup> On 28 June, in the quarter-finals of the tournament, Agüero assisted <a href="/wiki/Lautaro_Mart%C3%ADnez" title="Lautaro Martínez">Lautaro Martínez</a>'s opening goal, and was also involved in the second goal, scored by <a href="/wiki/Giovani_Lo_Celso" title="Giovani Lo Celso">Giovani Lo Celso</a>, as Argentina defeated Venezuela 2–0 to advance to the semi-finals.<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">&#91;225&#93;</a></sup> In the third-place match against Chile on 6 July, Agüero scored the opening goal in an eventual 2–1 win, to help Argentina capture the bronze medal.<sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">&#91;226&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span></h2>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:33%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">Sergio is a photocopy of <a href="/wiki/Rom%C3%A1rio" title="Romário">Romário</a>, they are the same player</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">— <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Mancini" title="Roberto Mancini">Roberto Mancini</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Romário_227-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Romário-227">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Often considered to be one of the best <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">strikers</a> in the world,<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">&#91;228&#93;</a></sup> Agüero is regarded as an all-out <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Centre-forward" title="Forward (association football)">centre forward</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">&#91;229&#93;</a></sup> although he is a versatile player, who can also play as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Second_striker" title="Forward (association football)">second striker</a> off another striker, which he often did at Atlético Madrid with <a href="/wiki/Diego_Forl%C3%A1n" title="Diego Forlán">Diego Forlán</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-milli_230-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-milli-230">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-versatility_231-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-versatility-231">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup> due to his passing ability, link-up play, tactical intelligence, and vision, which made him a capable assist-man.<sup id="cite_ref-versatility_231-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-versatility-231">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Aguero,_classe_da_vendere_232-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Aguero,_classe_da_vendere-232">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup> When asked to name the players who influenced his playing style, Agüero named former Brazilian striker <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronaldinho" title="Ronaldinho">Ronaldinho</a> and <a href="/wiki/Diego_Maradona" title="Diego Maradona">Diego Maradona</a> as the best players to have played the game, but said that the player who influenced his style of play the most was “the Brazilian Ronaldo”.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233">&#91;233&#93;</a></sup> Aguero has a diminutive figure with a stocky build, which has led to comparisons with former Manchester City teammate <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Tevez" title="Carlos Tevez">Carlos Tevez</a><sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">&#91;234&#93;</a></sup> and past <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forwards</a> such as <a href="/wiki/Rom%C3%A1rio" title="Romário">Romário</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Romário_227-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Romário-227">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Alessandro_Del_Piero" title="Alessandro Del Piero">Del Piero</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Aguero,_classe_da_vendere_232-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Aguero,_classe_da_vendere-232">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup> and Diego Maradona.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPN_Profile_235-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPN_Profile-235">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">&#91;236&#93;</a></sup> When both were on the same team, some pundits called Agüero Tevez's heir apparent at City<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup> and others said that he was superior to his compatriot.<sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238">&#91;238&#93;</a></sup> His ex-manager at Manchester City, <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Mancini" title="Roberto Mancini">Roberto Mancini</a>, has compared Agüero to former Brazilian striker, Romário, due to his pace, goalscoring ability, positioning in the area, and technique.<sup id="cite_ref-Romário_227-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Romário-227">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup> Although naturally right footed, Agüero is also capable of striking well with his left foot, and can finish well both inside and outside the area with his powerful and accurate shot.<sup id="cite_ref-Aguero,_classe_da_vendere_232-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Aguero,_classe_da_vendere-232">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPN_Profile_235-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPN_Profile-235">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A prolific goalscorer, Agüero's playing style is characterised by agility, acceleration and strength, being described as "sharp and clever" by former Argentine player <a href="/wiki/Osvaldo_Ardiles" title="Osvaldo Ardiles">Osvaldo Ardiles</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">&#91;239&#93;</a></sup> a view which is shared by his international captain Lionel Messi, who believes Agüero possesses "immense power, strength and an incredible work ethic."<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Combined with his close control, quick feet, <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> skills, and strength to keep the ball, he has been described as "a menace in the box".<sup id="cite_ref-milli_230-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-milli-230">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPN_Profile_235-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPN_Profile-235">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup> Despite his ability, Agüero's playing time has often been limited by injuries throughout his career.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPN_Profile_235-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPN_Profile-235">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_2011-09-08_001.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_2011-09-08_001.jpg/220px-Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_2011-09-08_001.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_2011-09-08_001.jpg/330px-Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_2011-09-08_001.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_2011-09-08_001.jpg/440px-Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_2011-09-08_001.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3543" data-file-height="2657" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero_2011-09-08_001.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Publicity photo for <a href="/wiki/Puma_AG" class="mw-redirect" title="Puma AG">Puma AG</a>, September 2011</div></div></div>
<p>Agüero was married to Gianinna Maradona, the youngest daughter of late Argentine footballer <a href="/wiki/Diego_Maradona" title="Diego Maradona">Diego Maradona</a>. On 19 February 2009, Gianinna gave birth to their son, Benjamín, in <a href="/wiki/Madrid" title="Madrid">Madrid</a>. Diego Maradona was there for the birth of his first grandson, while Agüero, then 20, missed Atlético's training session earlier in the day. Atlético offered their congratulations in a statement on their official website.<sup id="cite_ref-240" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-240">&#91;240&#93;</a></sup> Agüero and Gianinna separated in 2012 after four years together.<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">&#91;241&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Agüero's nickname "Kun", which features on his shirt, dates back to his childhood. It was first given to him by his grandparents,<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> due to a resemblance to the character "<a href="/wiki/Kum-Kum" title="Kum-Kum">Kum-Kum</a>" from the anime <a href="/wiki/Wanpaku_Omukashi_Kumu_Kumu" class="mw-redirect" title="Wanpaku Omukashi Kumu Kumu">Wanpaku Omukashi Kumu Kumu</a> which was Agüero's favourite television programme as a child.<sup id="cite_ref-kun_242-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kun-242">&#91;242&#93;</a></sup> He stated, "I have grown to appreciate it because it's unique. It's not every day an athlete is nicknamed after a cartoon character!"<sup id="cite_ref-kun_242-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kun-242">&#91;242&#93;</a></sup> Agüero has a tattoo on the inside of his right arm inscribed in <a href="/wiki/Tengwar" title="Tengwar">Tengwar</a>—a form of writing invented by <a href="/wiki/J._R._R._Tolkien" title="J. R. R. Tolkien">J. R. R. Tolkien</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Lord_of_the_Rings" title="The Lord of the Rings">The Lord of the Rings</a></i>—that transliterates roughly to <i>Kun Agüero</i> in the <a href="/wiki/Latin_script" title="Latin script">Latin script</a>. He also has a tattoo on his left arm of his son's name and date of birth.<sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243">&#91;243&#93;</a></sup> Agüero holds <a href="/wiki/Spanish_nationality_law" title="Spanish nationality law">Spanish nationality</a>, after being granted citizenship in 2010 whilst playing for <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-244" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-244">&#91;244&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Agüero shares a close friendship with <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>, his regular roommate during outings for the national team since 2005. He described Messi as being "like a brother" in his 2014 autobiography, <i>Born to Rise</i>, which contains a foreword written by Messi.<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">&#91;245&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Gast%C3%B3n_del_Castillo" title="Gastón del Castillo">Gastón del Castillo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mauricio_del_Castillo" title="Mauricio del Castillo">Mauricio del Castillo</a> are brothers of Agüero.<sup id="cite_ref-Brothers_246-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Brothers-246">&#91;246&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the three month football break due to the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic" title="COVID-19 pandemic">Coronavirus pandemic</a> in 2020, Agüero started live-streaming himself playing various videogames on <a href="/wiki/Twitch_(service)" title="Twitch (service)">Twitch</a>. He became the fastest-growing streamer in the month of May,<sup id="cite_ref-247" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-247">&#91;247&#93;</a></sup> reaching 1 million followers. He has been especially popular among the Hispanic community, collaborating with many big names such as <a href="/wiki/El_Rubius" title="El Rubius">El Rubius</a> and even calling Messi once live on air.<sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248">&#91;248&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
